name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:19 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 21, 2024
msg:When entering the door, my eldest son walked in a hurry, and ended up getting his sister's hands and feet stuck in the revolving door. My sister was only 5 years old, and the door sensor might not have sensed it. The lobby manager of the store came out immediately to deal with it, and called the engineer to come over immediately to deal with it. I observed carefully, and fortunately, the revolving door was designed with rubber buffers, so I pulled it out with a little force, and I didn't hurt my body much, which was lucky. Anyway, it was not a big deal, and I thought it was just like that. But what I didn't expect was that the lobby manager quickly sent a fruit bowl to apologize after we checked in (the content of the fruit bowl was quite rich, and I forgot to take a photo). Because it was not a big deal, and the main responsibility was on our side, we said it was unnecessary. But the hotel representative still said a lot of apologies, which made us embarrassed. Then, what I didn't expect was that when we checked out, the store also prepared two small gifts for the children. Of course, the children were very happy, and we adults were naturally grateful. In addition, because it was the last day of the trip, there were many items, so I asked their luggage waiter to help with SF Express, and took out 20 yuan to express my gratitude, but the hotel lobby manager and the waiters refused. Judging from these two small things, this hotel is still worth recommending.
Let's talk about the equipment and facilities in the room. There is an air purifier. There are anti-collision stickers on the corners, there are 2 wash basins, and the hair dryer is a high-speed hair dryer. These are all worthy of praise.
Slightly talking about the shortcomings, that is, since it is a family room, can you put an extra cabinet under the TV and a few more clothes hangers in the wardrobe.
